PUBLIC NOTICES
At the General Body meeting of SIDDHA SAMAJ, held at Vatakara Siddha Samaj Head Office (Siddhasramam,
Vatakara). On 1st October 2016, As per Section 222 of Siddha Samaj rules Brahmasri S. Sanandan has been elected
as the new General Representative of Siddha Samaj in the place of Brahmasri S. Bhakthavalsalan, the then General
Representative since Siddha Samaj on 5th October 2016.
It is, therefore notified to all that since 5th October 2016 onwards the whole authority and liability of General
Representative with respect to Siddha Samaj, assets, Etc., as per Siddha Samaj rules, is vested with the said
at Brahmasri S. Sanandan.
For Siddha Samaj
S. SAVYASACHI
(General President)
Siddhasramam, Ammampalayam,
Salem-636 141,
2nd November 2016.

S. ARUNAGIRI NATHAN,
(General Secretary).

R. Narasimhan a male child born to K. Ramaswamy on 7th May 1959, residing at No. 3-2, Block 1BX, AIR-INDIA
STAFF HOUSING COLONY, MEENAMBAKKAM, CHENNAI-600 027, has been living as a female after an elaborate
Sexual reassignment Surgery by. Dr. V. Dhamodara Raj, M.B.B.S. DNB. (Gen. Surg.) Mch., (Plastic Surgery)
Reg. No. 57161 TAMIL NADU MEDICAL COUNCIL). By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be
known as Ms. SINDHU NARASIMHAN. R.
Chennai,
3rd November 2016.

R. NARASIMHAN,

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
